city: string; state: string; zip: string };\n  onChange: (address: any) => void;\n  onNext: () => void;\n}\n\nconst VendorAddress: React.FC<Props> = ({ address, onChange, onNext }) => {\n  const [form, setForm] = useState(address);\n\n  const updateField = (field: string, value: string) => {\n    const updated = { ...form, [field]: value };\n    setForm(updated);\n    onChange(updated);\n  };\n\n  const isComplete = form.street && form.city && form.state && form.zip;\n\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    if ((cmd.includes('next') || cmd.includes('continue') || cmd.includes('save')) && isComplete) {\n      speak('Saving your address.', () => onNext());\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('skip')) {\n      speak('Skipping address for now.', () => onNext());\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset')) {\n      setForm({ street: '', city: '', state: '', zip: '' });\n      onChange({ street: '', city: '', state: '', zip: '' });\n      speak('Address cleared.');\n    }\n  }, [isComplete, onNext, onChange]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    return onCommand(handleCommand);\n  }, [handleCommand]);\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udccd</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\n        Business Address\n      </h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\n        Where is your business located?\n      </p>\n\n      <div style={{ maxWidth: '400px', margin: '0 auto', textAlign: 'left' }}>\n        <input\n          type=\"text\"\n          placeholder=\"Street Address\"\n          value={form.street}\n          onChange={e => updateField('street', e.target.value)}\n          style={{\n            width: '100%',\n            padding: '14px 16px',\n            marginBottom: '12px',\n            borderRadius: '10px',\n            border: `2px solid ${form.street ? '#B8860B' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n            color: '#fff',\n            fontSize: '1em'\n          }}\n        />\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '12px' }}>\n          <input\n            type=\"text\"\n            placeholder=\"City\"\n            value={form.city}\n            onChange={e => updateField('city', e.target.value)}\n            style={{\n              flex: 2,\n              padding: '14px 16px',\n              borderRadius: '10px',\n              border: `2px solid ${form.city ? '#B8860B' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\n              background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n              color: '#fff',\n              fontSize: '1em'\n            }}\n          />\n          <input\n            type=\"text\"\n            placeholder=\"State\"\n            value={form.state}\n            onChange={e => updateField('state', e.target.value.toUpperCase().slice(0, 2))}\n            style={{\n              flex: 1,\n              padding: '14px 16px',\n              borderRadius: '10px',\n              border: `2px solid ${form.state ? '#B8860B' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\n              background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n              color: '#fff',\n              fontSize: '1em',\n              textTransform: 'uppercase'\n            }}\n          />\n        </div>\n        <input\n          type=\"text\"\n          placeholder=\"ZIP Code\"\n          value={form.zip}\n          onChange={e => updateField('zip', e.target.value.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 5))}\n          style={{\n            width: '50%',\n            padding: '14px 16px',\n            marginBottom: '24px',\n            borderRadius: '10px',\n            border: `2px solid ${form.zip ? '#B8860B' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n            color: '#fff',\n            fontSize: '1em'\n          }}\n        />\n      </div>\n\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', justifyContent: 'center' }}>\n        <button\n          onClick={() => speak('Skipping.', () => onNext())}\n          style={{\n            padding: '14px 28px',\n            background: 'transparent',\n            color: '#888',\n            border: '1px solid #555',\n            borderRadius: '24px',\n            cursor: 'pointer',\n            fontWeight: 600\n          }}\n        >\n          Skip for now\n        </button>\n        <button\n          onClick={() => isComplete && speak('Saving.', () => onNext())}\n          disabled={!isComplete}\n          style={{\n            padding: '14px 36px',\n            background: isComplete ? 'linear-gradient(135deg, #B8860B, #DAA520)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n            color: isComplete ? '#000' : '#555',\n            border: 'none',\n            borderRadius: '24px',\n            cursor: isComplete ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed',\n            fontWeight: 700\n          }}\n        >\n          Continue \u2192\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      <AgenticBar\n        context=\"Business Address\"\n        hints={['\"next\" to continue', '\"skip\" to skip']}\n        welcomeMessage=\"Enter your business address, or say skip to add it later.\"\n        autoStart={true}\n      />\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default VendorAddress;\nEOF\necho \"\u2705 VendorAddress.tsx created\"\n\n# Created ${result.stats?.totalProducts || 0} products from your catalog.   <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        Upload a PDF catalog to create your product listings\\n      </p>\\n\\n      {state.status === 'idle' && (\\n        <>\\n \\ud83d\\udcc1 Choose PDF File\\n          </button>\\n          <p style={{ color: '#666', marginTop: '16px', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n            or drag and drop your PDF here\\n          </p>\\n {state.stats.totalImages}\\n              </div>\\n              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Images</div>\\n            </div>\\n            <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' \\\"[APPLY] Creating VendorAddress.tsx...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$W/src/components/signin/vendor/VendorAddress.tsx\\\" << 'EOF'\\n// VendorAddress.tsx - Business Address with AgenticBar\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';\\nimport AgenticBar, { speak, onCommand } from '../../../agentic';\\n\\ninterface Props {\\n  address: { street: string; city: string; state: string; zip: string };\\n  onChange: (address: any) => void;\\n  onNext: () => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst VendorAddress: React.FC<Props> = ({ address, onChange, onNext }) => {\\n  const [form, setForm] = useState(address);\\n\\n  const updateField = (field: string, value: string) => {\\n    const updated = { ...form, [field]: value };\\n    setForm(updated);\\n    onChange(updated);\\n  };\\n\\n  const isComplete = form.street && form.city && form.state && form.zip;\\n\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    if ((cmd.includes('next') || cmd.includes('continue') || cmd.includes('save')) && isComplete) {\\n      speak('Saving your address.', () => onNext());\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('skip')) {\\n      speak('Skipping address for now.', () => onNext());\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset')) {\\n      setForm({ street: '', city: '', state: '', zip: '' });\\n      onChange({ street: '', city: '', state: '', zip: '' });\\n      speak('Address cleared.');\\n    }\\n  }, [isComplete, onNext, onChange]);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    return onCommand(handleCommand);\\n  }, [handleCommand]);\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udccd</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\\n        Business Address\\n      </h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        Where is your business located?\\n      </p>\\n\\n      <div style={{ maxWidth: '400px', margin: '0 auto', textAlign: 'left' }}>\\n        <input\\n          type=\\\"text\\\"\\n          placeholder=\\\"Street Address\\\"\\n          value={form.street}\\n          onChange={e => updateField('street', e.target.value)}\\n          style={{\\n            width: '100%',\\n            padding: '14px 16px',\\n            marginBottom: '12px',\\n            borderRadius: '10px',\\n            border: `2px solid ${form.street ? '#B8860B' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n            color: '#fff',\\n            fontSize: '1em'\\n          }}\\n        />\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '12px' }}>\\n          <input\\n            type=\\\"text\\\"\\n            placeholder=\\\"City\\\"\\n            value={form.city}\\n            onChange={e => updateField('city', e.target.value)}\\n            style={{\\n              flex: 2,\\n              padding: '14px 16px',\\n              borderRadius: '10px',\\n              border: `2px solid ${form.city ? \"[APPLY] Creating Teleprompter.tsx...\"\n\ncat > \"$W/src/agentic/Teleprompter.tsx\" << 'EOF'\n// Teleprompter.tsx - Shows what Mr. V is saying in real-time\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';\nimport { voiceBrain } from './VoiceBrain';\n\ninterface TeleprompterProps {\n  position?: 'top' | 'bottom' | 'center';\n  style?: 'minimal' | 'full' | 'caption';\n}\n\nconst Teleprompter: React.FC<TeleprompterProps> = ({ \n  position = 'bottom',\n  style = 'full'\n}) => {\n  const [currentText, setCurrentText] = useState('');\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\n  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);\n  const animationRef = useRef<number>();\n  const charIndexRef = useRef(0);\n\n  // Subscribe to speech events\n  useEffect(() => {\n    // Intercept speak function to get text\n    const originalSpeak = voiceBrain.sp.bind(voiceBrain);\n    \n    voiceBrain.sp = (text: string, onDone?: () => void) => {\n      if (text) {\n        setCurrentText(text);\n        setIsVisible(true);\n        charIndexRef.current = 0;\n        setDisplayText('');\n      }\n      originalSpeak(text, () => {\n        setTimeout(() => setIsVisible(false), 1000);\n        onDone?.();\n      });\n    };\n\n    return () => {\n      voiceBrain.sp = originalSpeak;\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  // Typewriter effect\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!currentText || !isVisible) return;\n\n    const animate = () => {\n      if (charIndexRef.current < currentText.length) {\n        setDisplayText(currentText.slice(0, charIndexRef.current + 1));\n        charIndexRef.current++;\n        animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(() => {\n          setTimeout(animate, 30); // Typing speed\n        });\n      }\n    };\n\n    animate();\n\n    return () => {\n      if (animationRef.current) {\n        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);\n      }\n    };\n  }, [currentText, isVisible]);\n\n  if (!isVisible || !displayText) return null;\n\n  const positionStyles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {\n    top: { top: '80px', left: '50%', transform: 'translateX(-50%)' },\n    bottom: { bottom: '100px', left: '50%', transform: 'translateX(-50%)' },\n    center: { top: '50%', left: '50%', transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)' }\n  };\n\n  const styleVariants: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {\n    minimal: {\n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)',\n      padding: '12px 24px',\n      borderRadius: '24px'\n    },\n    full: {\n      background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(20,20,20,0.95), rgba(40,40,40,0.95))',\n      padding: '20px 32px',\n      borderRadius: '16px',\n      border: '2px solid #B8860B',\n      boxShadow: '0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.4)'\n    },\n    caption: {\n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.85)',\n      padding: '16px 24px',\n      borderRadius: '8px',\n      maxWidth: '600px'\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      position: 'fixed',\n      zIndex: 99999,\n      ...positionStyles[position],\n      ...styleVariants[style],\n      animation: 'teleprompter-fade-in 0.3s ease'\n    }}>\n      {style === 'full' && (\n        <div style={{\n          display: 'flex',\n          alignItems: 'center',\n          gap: '12px',\n          marginBottom: '12px'\n        }}>\n          <span style={{\n            width: '40px',\n            height: '40px',\n            borderRadius: '50%',\n            background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #B8860B, #DAA520)',\n            display: 'flex',\n            alignItems: 'center',\n            justifyContent: 'center',\n            fontSize: '1.2em'\n          }}>\n            \ud83e\udd16\n          </span>\n          <div>\n            <div style={{ color: '#B8860B', fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Mr. V</div>\n            <div style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '0.75em' }}>Speaking...</div>\n          </div>\n          <span style={{\n            marginLeft: 'auto',\n            width: '12px',\n            height: '12px',\n            borderRadius: '50%',\n            background: '#4CAF50',\n            animation: 'teleprompter-pulse 1s infinite'\n          }} />\n        </div>\n      )}\n      \n      <div style={{\n        color: '#fff',\n        fontSize: style === 'caption' ? '1.1em' : '1.3em',\n        lineHeight: 1.5,\n        maxWidth: '500px',\n        textAlign: style === 'caption' ? 'center' : 'left'\n      }}>\n        {displayText}\n        <span style={{\n          display: 'inline-block',\n          width: '2px',\n          height: '1.2em',\n          background: '#B8860B',\n          marginLeft: '2px',\n          animation: 'teleprompter-cursor 0.5s infinite'\n        }} />\n      </div>\n\n      <style>{`\n        @keyframes teleprompter-fade-in {\n          from { 50% { opacity: 0; }\n        }\n      `}</style>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default Teleprompter;\nEOF\necho \"\u2705 Teleprompter.tsx created\"\n\n# key={i}\n              style={{\n                width: '3px',\n                background: config.color,\n                borderRadius: '2px',\n                animation: `waveform ${0.5 + i * 0.1}s 'caption';\\n}\\n\\nconst Teleprompter: React.FC<TeleprompterProps> = ({ \\n  position = 'bottom',\\n  style = 'full'\\n}) => {\\n  const [currentText, setCurrentText] = useState('');\\n  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState('');\\n  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);\\n  const animationRef = useRef<number>();\\n  const charIndexRef = useRef(0);\\n\\n  // Subscribe to speech events\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    // Intercept speak function to get text\\n    const originalSpeak = voiceBrain.sp.bind(voiceBrain);\\n    \\n    voiceBrain.sp = (text: string, onDone?: () => void) => {\\n      if (text) {\\n        setCurrentText(text);\\n        setIsVisible(true);\\n        charIndexRef.current = 0;\\n        setDisplayText('');\\n      }\\n      originalSpeak(text, () => {\\n        setTimeout(() => setIsVisible(false), 1000);\\n        onDone?.();\\n      });\\n    };\\n\\n    return () => {\\n      voiceBrain.sp = originalSpeak;\\n    };\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Typewriter effect\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!currentText || !isVisible) return;\\n\\n    const animate = () => {\\n      if (charIndexRef.current < currentText.length) {\\n        setDisplayText(currentText.slice(0, charIndexRef.current + 1));\\n        charIndexRef.current++;\\n        animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(() => {\\n          setTimeout(animate, 30); // Typing speed\\n        });\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    animate();\\n\\n    return () => {\\n      if (animationRef.current) {\\n        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);\\n      }\\n    };\\n  }, [currentText, isVisible]);\\n\\n  if (!isVisible || !displayText) return null;\\n\\n  const positionStyles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {\\n    top: { top: '80px', left: '50%', };\\n\\n  const styleVariants: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {\\n    minimal: {\\n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)',\\n      padding: '12px 24px',\\n      borderRadius: '24px'\\n    },\\n }\\n  };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{\\n      position: 'fixed',\\n      zIndex: 99999,\\n      ...positionStyles[position],\\n      ...styleVariants[style],\\n      animation: 'teleprompter-fade-in 0.3s ease'\\n    }}>\\n      {style === 'full' && (\\n        <div style={{\\n          display: 'flex',\\n          alignItems: 'center',\\n          gap: '12px',\\n          marginBottom: '12px'\\n        }}>\\n          <span style={{\\n            width: '40px',\\n            height: '40px',\\n            borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #B8860B, #DAA520)',\\n            display: 'flex',\\n            alignItems: 'center',\\n            justifyContent: 'center',\\n            fontSize: '1.2em'\\n          }}>\\n            \\ud83e\\udd16\\n          </span>\\n          <div>\\n            <div style={{ color: '#B8860B', fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Mr. V</div>\\n            <div style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '0.75em' }}>Speaking...</div>\\n          </div>\\n          <span style={{\\n            marginLeft: 'auto',\\n            width: '12px',\\n            height: '12px',\\n            borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: '#4CAF50',\\n            animation: 'teleprompter-pulse 1s infinite'\\n          }} />\\n        </div>\\n      )}\\n      \\n      <div 'center' : 'left'\\n      }}>\\n        {displayText}\\n        <span style={{\\n          display: 'inline-block',\\n          width: '2px',\\n          height: '1.2em',\\n          background: 'react';\\nimport { useVoice } from './AgenticBar';\\n\\ninterface StatusIndicatorProps {\\n  size?: 'small' | 'medium' | 'large';\\n  showLabel?: boolean;\\n  showWaveform?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\nconst StatusIndicator: React.FC<StatusIndicatorProps> = ({\\n  size = 'medium',\\n  showLabel = true,\\n  showWaveform = true\\n}) => {\\n  const voice = useVoice();\\n  \\n  const sizes = {\\n    small: { SPEAKING: { color: '#FFD700', icon: '\\ud83d\\udd0a', label: 'Speaking' },\\n    PAUSED: { color: '#FF9800', icon: '\\u23f8\\ufe0f', label: 'Paused' },\\n    THINKING: { color: '#2196F3', icon: '\\ud83e\\udd14', label: 'Thinking' }\\n  };\\n\\n  const config = stateConfig[voice.audioState] || stateConfig.IDLE;\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{\\n      display: 'inline-flex',\\n      alignItems: 'center',\\n      gap: '8px'\\n    }}>\\n      {/* Main Indicator */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        position: 'relative',\\n        width: s.indicator,\\n        height: s.indicator\\n      }}>\\n        <span style={{\\n          display: 'block',\\n          width: '100%',\\n          height: '100%',\\n          borderRadius: '50%',\\n          background: config.color,\\n            position: 'absolute',\\n            top: 0,\\n            left: 0,\\n            width: '100%',\\n            height: '100%',\\n            borderRadius: '50%',\\n            border: `2px solid ${config.color}`,\\n            animation: 'status-ripple 1.5s infinite'\\n          }} />\\n        )}\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {/* Waveform */}\\n      {showWaveform && (voice.isListening || voice.isSpeaking) && (\\n        <div style={{\\n          display: 'flex',\\n          alignItems: 'center',\\n          gap: '2px',\\n          height: s.waveHeight\\n        }}>\\n file\n    // For now, create a mock scene graph for Skyven building\n    this.sceneGraph = {\n      objects: [],\n      floors: Array.from({ length: 50 }, (_, i) => ({\n        number: i + 1,\n        id: `floor_${i + 1}`,\n        label: `Floor ${i + 1}`\n      })),\n      hotspots: [\n        { id: 'lobby', label: 'Lobby', position: [0, 0, 0] },\n        { id: 'amenities', label: 'Amenities', [-20, 3, 0] }\n      ],\n      cameraPresets: [\n        { id: 'exterior', label: 'Exterior View' },\n        { id: 'interior', label: 'Interior View' },\n        { id: 'aerial', label: 'Aerial View' },\n        { id: 'street', label: 'Street View' }\n      ]\n    };\n\n    console.log('[GLBScene] Scene graph built:', this.sceneGraph.floors.length, 'floors');\n  }\n\n  // Go to specific floor\n  async goToFloor(floorNumber: number): Promise<boolean> {\n    if (!this.sceneGraph) {\n      speak('Scene not loaded yet.');\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    const floor = this.sceneGraph.floors.find(f => f.number === floorNumber);\n    if (!floor) {\n      speak(`Floor ${floorNumber} not found. This building has floors 1 to ${this.sceneGraph.floors.length}.`);\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    console.log('[GLBScene] Going to floor:', floorNumber);\n    \n    // Animate to floor (would call ${floorNumber}.`);\n    \n    // Dispatch event for UI updates\n    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('glb-floor-change', { \n      detail: { floor: floorNumber } \n    }));\n    \n    return true;\n  }\n\n  // Go to hotspot\n  async goToHotspot(hotspotId: string): Promise<boolean> {\n    if (!this.sceneGraph) return false;\n\n    const hotspot = this.sceneGraph.hotspots.find(h => \n      h.id === hotspotId || h.label.toLowerCase().includes(hotspotId.toLowerCase())\n    );\n    \n    if (!hotspot) {\n      speak(`${hotspotId} not found in this building.`);\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    console.log('[GLBScene] Going to hotspot:', hotspot.label);\n    \n    if (this.viewerAPI?.focusHotspot) {\n      this.viewerAPI.focusHotspot(hotspot.id);\n    }\n    \n    speak(`Going to // Process voice command for GLB\n  async processCommand(text: string): Promise<boolean> {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n\n    // Floor navigation: \"go to floor 44\", \"floor 12\", \"44th this.setCameraPreset('exterior');\n    }\n    if (lower.includes('interior') || lower.includes('inside')) {\n      return this.setCameraPreset('interior');\n    }\n    if (lower.includes('aerial') || lower.includes('bird')) {\n      return this.setCameraPreset('aerial');\n    }\n    if (lower.includes('street')) {\n      return this.setCameraPreset('street');\n    }\n\n    // Floor navigation shortcuts\n    if (lower.includes('top floor') || lower.includes('penthouse')) {\n      return this.goToFloor(this.sceneGraph?.floors.length || 50);\n    }\n    if (lower.includes('ground') || lower.includes('first floor')) {\n      return this.goToFloor(1);\n    }\n    if (lower.includes('up') || lower.includes('next floor')) {\n      return this.goToFloor(this.currentFloor + 1);\n    }\n    if (lower.includes('down') || lower.includes('previous floor')) {\n      return this.goToFloor(Math.max(1, this.currentFloor - 1));\n    }\n\n    return false;\n  }\n}\n\nexport const
